2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 The library can be installed with the appropriate command below:
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 * For CUDA 11, run:    conda install cudatoolkit cuda-version=11
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 * For CUDA 12, run:    conda install cuda-cudart cuda-version=12
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 To enable CUDA support, please follow UCX's instruction above.
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 To additionally enable NCCL support, run:    conda install nccl
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 On Linux, Open MPI is built with CUDA awareness but it is disabled by default.
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 To enable it, please set the environment variable
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 OMPI_MCA_opal_cuda_support=true
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 before launching your MPI processes.
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 Equivalently, you can set the MCA parameter in the command line:
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 mpiexec --mca opal_cuda_support 1 ...
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 Note that you might also need to set UCX_MEMTYPE_CACHE=n for CUDA awareness via
2024-12-19T20:08:25Z #11 175.7 UCX. Please consult UCX documentation for further details.
